2025-09-14 13:06:25.165 | INFO     | metagpt.roles.di.role_zero:_act:294 - Commands outputs: 
Command Engineer2.write_new_code executed: The file /home/mas-metagpt/Desktop/MetaGPT/workspace/src/App.jsx has been successfully created, with content:
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import LanguageSelector from './components/LanguageSelector';
import CodeEditor from './components/CodeEditor';
import OutputDisplay from './components/OutputDisplay';
import LanguageHandler from './utils/LanguageHandler';

const App = () => {
    const [language, setLanguage] = useState('Python');
    const [code, setCode] = useState('');
    const [output, setOutput] = useState('');

    const handleLanguageChange = (selectedLanguage) => {
        setLanguage(selectedLanguage);
    };

    const handleCodeChange = (newCode) => {
        setCode(newCode);
    };

    const executeCode = async () => {
        const languageHandler = new LanguageHandler();
        const result = await languageHandler.execute_code(language, code);
        setOutput(result);
    };

    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Programming Assignment System</h1>
            <LanguageSelector onLanguageChange={handleLanguageChange} />
            <CodeEditor code={code} onCodeChange={handleCodeChange} />
            <button onClick={executeCode}>Run Code</button>
            <OutputDisplay output={output} />
        </div>
    );
};

export default App;

2025-09-14 13:06:31.452 | INFO     | metagpt.roles.di.role_zero:_act:294 - Commands outputs: 
Command Engineer2.write_new_code executed: The file /home/mas-metagpt/Desktop/MetaGPT/workspace/src/components/LanguageSelector.jsx has been successfully created, with content:
import React from 'react';

const LanguageSelector = ({ onLanguageChange }) => {
    const languages = ['Python', 'JavaScript', 'Java'];

    const handleChange = (event) => {
        onLanguageChange(event.target.value);
    };

    return (
        <div>
            <label htmlFor="language-select">Select Language:</label>
            <select id="language-select" onChange={handleChange}>
                {languages.map((language) => (
                    <option key={language} value={language}>
                        {language}
                    </option>
                ))}
            </select>
        </div>
    );
};

export default LanguageSelector;

If you keeping encountering errors, unexpected situation, or you are not sure of proceeding, use RoleZero.ask_human to ask for help.\n2. Carefully review your progress at the current task, if your actions so far has not fulfilled the task instruction, you should continue with current task. import React from 'react';

const CodeEditor = ({ code, onCodeChange }) => {
    const handleChange = (event) => {
        onCodeChange(event.target.value);
    };

    return (
        <div>
            <label htmlFor="code-editor">Code Editor:</label>
            <textarea
                id="code-editor"
                value={code}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows="10"
                cols="50"
                placeholder="Write your code here..."
            />
        </div>
    );
};

export default CodeEditor;

Command Engineer2.write_new_code executed: The file /home/mas-metagpt/Desktop/MetaGPT/workspace/src/utils/LanguageHandler.js has been successfully created, with content:
// src/utils/LanguageHandler.js

import PythonModule from './PythonModule';
import JavaScriptModule from './JavaScriptModule';
import JavaModule from './JavaModule';

class LanguageHandler {
    async execute_code(language, code) {
        let result;
        switch (language) {
            case 'Python':
                const pythonModule = new PythonModule();
                result = await pythonModule.run(code);
                break;
            case 'JavaScript':
                const jsModule = new JavaScriptModule();
                result = await jsModule.run(code);
                break;
            case 'Java':
                const javaModule = new JavaModule();
                result = await javaModule.run(code);
                break;
            default:
                throw new Error('Unsupported language');
        }
        return result;
    }
}

export default LanguageHandler;

Command Engineer2.write_new_code executed: The file /home/mas-metagpt/Desktop/MetaGPT/workspace/src/utils/PythonModule.js has been successfully created, with content:
// src/utils/PythonModule.js

class PythonModule {
    async run(code) {
        // Load Pyodide
        if (!window.pyodide) {
            await this.loadPyodide();
        }

        try {
            // Execute the Python code
            const result = await window.pyodide.runPythonAsync(code);
            return result;
        } catch (error) {
            return `Error: ${error.message}`;
        }
    }

    async loadPyodide() {
        // Load the Pyodide environment
        window.pyodide = await loadPyodide();
    }
}

export default PythonModule;
